def search_nested_data(obj, path=''):
findings = []
search_terms = ['artist', 'suffragette', 'clare', 'lavenham', 'notable', 'painter', 'activist']

if isinstance(obj, dict):
for key, value in obj.items():

findings.append({
'path': current_path,
'terms': found_terms,
'value': value[:200] + '...' if len(value) > 200 else value
})

# Recurse into nested structures
findings.extend(search_nested_data(value, current_path))

elif isinstance(obj, list):
for i, item in enumerate(obj):
current_path = f'{path}[{i}]' if path else f'[{i}]'
findings.extend(search_nested_data(item, current_path))

elif isinstance(obj, str):
obj_lower = obj.lower()
found_terms = [term for term in search_terms if term in obj_lower]
if found_terms:
findings.append({
'path': path,
'terms': found_terms,
'value': obj[:200] + '...' if len(obj) > 200 else obj
})

return findings

file_size = os.path.getsize(suffolk_path)
print(f' File size: {file_size:,} bytes')

if suffolk_file.endswith('.json'):
with open(suffolk_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
raw_content = f.read()

try:
data = json.loads(raw_content)
print(f' ‚úÖ JSON parsed successfully - Type: {type(data).__name__}')

# Quick search for relevant terms
content_str = json.dumps(data, ensure_ascii=False).lower()
search_terms = ['artist', 'suffragette', 'clare', 'lavenham', 'notable']
found_terms = [term for term in search_terms if term in content_str]

if found_terms:
print(f' üéØ Found terms: {found_terms}')
# Show relevant parts
if isinstance(data, dict):
for key, value in data.items():
if isinstance(value, str) and any(term in value.lower() for term in found_terms):
print(f' Key "{key}": {value[:150]}...' if len(str(value)) > 150 else f' Key "{key}": {value}')
else:
print(f' ‚ùå No relevant terms found')

except json.JSONDecodeError:
print(' ‚ùå JSON parsing failed')

else:
# Text file
with open(suffolk_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
content = f.read()

content_lower = content.lower()
search_terms = ['artist', 'suffragette', 'clare', 'lavenham', 'notable']
found_terms = [term for term in search_terms if term in content_lower]

if found_terms:
print(f' üéØ Found terms: {found_terms}')
# Show relevant lines
lines = content.split('\n')
for i, line in enumerate(lines):
if any(term in line.lower() for term in found_terms):
print(f' Line {i+1}: {line.strip()}')
else:
print(' ‚ùå No relevant terms found')

except Exception as e:
print(f' ‚ùå Error analyzing {suffolk_file}: {str(e)}')

print()

print('\n=== STEP 5: SUMMARY AND CONCLUSION ===\n')

print('WORKSPACE ANALYSIS COMPLETE:')
print(f'‚Ä¢ Total files analyzed: {len(workspace_files)}')
print(f'‚Ä¢ Relevant files identified: {len(relevant_files)}')
print(f'‚Ä¢ Clare-specific files: {len(clare_files)}')
print(f'‚Ä¢ Artist-related files: {len(artist_files)}')
print(f'‚Ä¢ Suffolk-specific files: {len(suffolk_files)}')
print(f'‚Ä¢ Comprehensive files: {len(comprehensive_files)}')

if clare_files:
print(f'\nüéØ PRIORITY ANALYSIS: Clare file "{clare_files[0]}" examined')
elif comprehensive_files:
print(f'\nüéØ FALLBACK ANALYSIS: Comprehensive file examined')
else:
print('\n‚ùì No priority files found for analysis')

print('\n=== FINAL STATUS ===\n')
print('Based on systematic workspace file analysis:')
if clare_files or any('artist' in f.lower() or 'suffragette' in f.lower() for f in comprehensive_files):
print('‚úÖ Found files likely containing artist-suffragette information')
print('üìã Specific identity should be extracted from analyzed file contents above')
print('üéØ Ready to identify the notable artist-suffragette from Lavenham')
else:
print('‚ùì No specific artist-suffragette information found in existing files')
print('üîç May need targeted web research for Lavenham notable residents')
print('üìö Historical records search required for 17th-century Lavenham artists/suffragettes')

print('\n=== WORKSPACE FILE ANALYSIS COMPLETE ===\n')
print('All relevant files have been systematically inspected and analyzed')

### Development Step 50: Locate 17th-Century Ghost Army Texts, Identify Suffolk Supernatural Sites, and Find Suffragette Artists

**Description**: Search for historical documents from the 17th century that record both a spectral army apparition in Ireland and supernatural events in Britain, focusing on identifying works like Joseph Glanvill's 'Saducismus Triumphatus' (1681) or similar collections of supernatural accounts. These compilations often documented multiple paranormal events across different locations. Once the specific document is identified, locate any Suffolk locations mentioned in connection with unusual supernatural events, then research notable individuals from that actual Suffolk place who were both artists and suffragettes.

**Use Cases**:
- Early modern folklore researcher compiling and cross-referencing 17th-century Irish and British apparition narratives to support a PhD thesis on transnational spectral traditions
- Digital humanities lab automating batch retrieval and OCR processing of historical occult manuscripts from Internet Archive to build a searchable corpus of 17th-century supernatural accounts
- Curator team mapping paranormal sites mentioned in Saducismus Triumphatus for a Suffolk-themed exhibition on local ghost lore and suffragette artists in regional museums
- Genealogist service tracing Suffolk-born women advocates who were both suffragettes and artists by correlating historical parish records with supernatural event locations documented in Glanvill‚Äôs works
- Small press specializing in reprints of public domain esoteric texts using automated searches to identify viable editions of Saducismus Triumphatus and extract contextual metadata for new annotated volumes
- Heritage tourism operator designing a guided ghost-walk in Suffolk by pinpointing real 17th-century haunted locales from primary sources and promoting stories of local female artists-activists
- University history department setting up a teaching module where students script-driven scrape Internet Archive to analyze the geographic distribution of witchcraft and hauntings in 17th-century Britain

```
import os
import requests
import json
import time
from urllib.parse import quote_plus
from bs4 import BeautifulSoup

print('=== INTERNET ARCHIVE SEARCH FOR SADUCISMUS TRIUMPHATUS ===')
print('Switching to Internet Archive to access actual historical documents')
print('Previous Google searches were blocked - using archive.org for direct text access\n')

# Ensure workspace directory exists
os.makedirs('workspace', exist_ok=True)

# Initialize results storage
archive_results = {
'timestamp': time.strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'),
'method': 'Internet Archive direct access',
'objective': 'Find Saducismus Triumphatus and 17th century supernatural texts with Suffolk connections',
'searches': [],
'documents_found': [],
'suffolk_references': [],
'analysis': {}
}

print('TARGET: Joseph Glanvill\'s "Saducismus Triumphatus" (1681)')
print('GOAL: Find Suffolk locations mentioned in supernatural contexts')
print('FINAL GOAL: Identify artists/suffragettes from those Suffolk places\n')

# Headers for Internet Archive requests
headers = {
'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/91.0.4472.124 Safari/537.36',
'Accept': 'text/html,application/xhtml+xml,application/xml;q=0.9,*/*;q=0.8'
}

print('=== PHASE 1: DIRECT INTERNET ARCHIVE SEARCH ===')
print('=' * 60)

# Search Internet Archive for Saducismus Triumphatus
archive_queries = [
'Saducismus Triumphatus Glanvill',
'Joseph Glanvill supernatural',
'Saducismus Triumphatus 1681',
'17th century supernatural Britain Ireland'
]

for i, query in enumerate(archive_queries, 1):
print(f'\nInternet Archive Search {i}: {query}')
print('-' * 50)

try:
# Search Internet Archive
archive_search_url = f'https://archive.org/search.php?query={quote_plus(query)}'
print(f'URL: {archive_search_url}')

response = requests.get(archive_search_url, headers=headers, timeout=30)
print(f'Status: {response.status_code}')

if response.status_code == 200:
# Save search results
filename = f'archive_search_{i}_{query.replace(" ", "_")}.html'
filepath = os.path.join('workspace', filename)

with open(filepath, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
f.write(response.text)

print(f'Saved: {filepath}')

# Parse search results
soup = BeautifulSoup(response.text, 'html.parser')

# Look for Internet Archive result items
result_items = soup.find_all(['div', 'article'], class_=lambda x: x and 'item' in str(x).lower())
if not result_items:
result_items = soup.find_all('a', href=lambda x: x and '/details/' in str(x))

print(f'Found {len(result_items)} potential results')

relevant_results = []
for j, item in enumerate(result_items[:10], 1):
try:
# Extract title and link
title_elem = item.find(['h3', 'h4', 'span', 'a']) or item
title = title_elem.get_text().strip() if title_elem else 'No title'

link_elem = item.find('a', href=True) or (item if item.name == 'a' else None)
link = link_elem.get('href') if link_elem else 'No link'

# Make link absolute if relative
if link.startswith('/details/'):
link = f'https://archive.org{link}'

# Check relevance
combined_text = f'{title} {link}'.lower()

relevance_indicators = []
if 'glanvill' in combined_text: relevance_indicators.append('glanvill')
if 'saducismus' in combined_text: relevance_indicators.append('saducismus')
if 'triumphatus' in combined_text: relevance_indicators.append('triumphatus')
if 'supernatural' in combined_text: relevance_indicators.append('supernatural')
if '1681' in combined_text: relevance_indicators.append('1681')
if 'witchcraft' in combined_text: relevance_indicators.append('witchcraft')

if relevance_indicators or len(title) > 10:
print(f' {j}. {title[:80]}...')
if relevance_indicators:
print(f' ‚≠ê Relevant terms: {', '.join(relevance_indicators)}')
print(f' Link: {link}')

relevant_results.append({
'title': title,
'link': link,
'relevance_terms': relevance_indicators,
'query': query
})

except Exception as e:
continue

archive_results['searches'].append({
'query': query,
'results_count': len(relevant_results),
'results': relevant_results,
'html_file': filepath
})

# If we found highly relevant results, mark them
high_relevance = [r for r in relevant_results if
any(term in r['relevance_terms'] for term in ['glanvill', 'saducismus', 'triumphatus'])]

if high_relevance:
print(f'\nüéØ HIGH RELEVANCE DOCUMENTS FOUND: {len(high_relevance)}')
archive_results['documents_found'].extend(high_relevance)

for doc in high_relevance:
print(f' üìö {doc["title"]}')
print(f' Terms: {', '.join(doc["relevance_terms"])}')
print(f' Link: {doc["link"]}')

else:
print(f'Failed with status {response.status_code}')

except Exception as e:
print(f'Error: {str(e)}')

time.sleep(2) # Rate limiting

print('\n' + '=' * 80)
print('PHASE 2: ANALYZING INTERNET ARCHIVE FINDINGS')
print('=' * 80)

total_documents = len(archive_results['documents_found'])
print(f'Total relevant documents found: {total_documents}')

if archive_results['documents_found']:
print('\nüìö DOCUMENT ANALYSIS:')
print('-' * 40)

# Sort by relevance (number of matching terms)
archive_results['documents_found'].sort(
key=lambda x: len(x['relevance_terms']), reverse=True
)

for i, doc in enumerate(archive_results['documents_found'], 1):
print(f'\n{i}. {doc["title"]}')
print(f' Relevance terms: {', '.join(doc["relevance_terms"])}')
print(f' Query: {doc["query"]}')
print(f' Archive link: {doc["link"]}')

# If this looks like Saducismus Triumphatus, try to access it
if any(term in doc['relevance_terms'] for term in ['saducismus', 'glanvill']):
print(f' üéØ POTENTIAL TARGET DOCUMENT - Will attempt to access content')

print('\n=== PHASE 3: ACCESSING SADUCISMUS TRIUMPHATUS CONTENT ===')
print('=' * 70)

# Try to access the most relevant document directly
if archive_results['documents_found']:
top_document = archive_results['documents_found'][0]
print(f'Attempting to access: {top_document["title"]}')
print(f'Link: {top_document["link"]}')

try:
# Try to access the document page
doc_response = requests.get(top_document['link'], headers=headers, timeout=30)
print(f'Document page status: {doc_response.status_code}')

if doc_response.status_code == 200:
# Save document page
doc_filename = 'saducismus_triumphatus_archive_page.html'
doc_filepath = os.path.join('workspace', doc_filename)

with open(doc_filepath, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
f.write(doc_response.text)

print(f'Document page saved: {doc_filepath}')

# Parse for text access links
doc_soup = BeautifulSoup(doc_response.text, 'html.parser')

# Look for text/PDF download links
text_links = []
for link in doc_soup.find_all('a', href=True):
href = link.get('href')
link_text = link.get_text().lower()

if any(format_type in href.lower() for format_type in ['.txt', '.pdf', '/stream/', 'text']):
text_links.append({
'text': link_text,
'href': href,
'full_url': href if href.startswith('http') else f'https://archive.org{href}'
})

print(f'\nFound {len(text_links)} potential text access links:')
for i, link in enumerate(text_links[:5], 1):
print(f' {i}. {link["text"][:50]}... -> {link["href"]}')

# Try to access text content if available
if text_links:
text_link = text_links[0] # Try first text link
print(f'\nAttempting to access text content: {text_link["full_url"]}')

try:
text_response = requests.get(text_link['full_url'], headers=headers, timeout=30)
print(f'Text access status: {text_response.status_code}')

if text_response.status_code == 200:
# Save text content
text_filename = 'saducismus_triumphatus_text_content.txt'
text_filepath = os.path.join('workspace', text_filename)

with open(text_filepath, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
f.write(text_response.text)

print(f'‚úÖ TEXT CONTENT SAVED: {text_filepath}')
print(f'Content length: {len(text_response.text):,} characters')

# Quick analysis for Suffolk mentions
text_content = text_response.text.lower()

if 'suffolk' in text_content:
print('\nüéØ SUFFOLK FOUND IN TEXT! Extracting references...')

# Find Suffolk contexts
sentences = text_content.split('.')
suffolk_contexts = []

for sentence in sentences:
if 'suffolk' in sentence and len(sentence.strip()) > 10:
suffolk_contexts.append(sentence.strip()[:300])

print(f'Found {len(suffolk_contexts)} Suffolk references:')
for i, context in enumerate(suffolk_contexts[:3], 1):
print(f' {i}. {context}...')

archive_results['suffolk_references'] = suffolk_contexts
else:
print('\n‚ùå No Suffolk references found in this text')
print('Will need to search for other 17th century supernatural compilations')

# Show sample of content
print('\nüìÑ SAMPLE CONTENT (first 500 characters):')
print('-' * 50)
print(text_response.text[:500])
print('-' * 50)

except Exception as e:
print(f'Error accessing text content: {str(e)}')

except Exception as e:
print(f'Error accessing document: {str(e)}')

else:
print('‚ùå No relevant documents found in Internet Archive search')
print('Will need to try alternative historical document repositories')

# Save comprehensive results
results_file = os.path.join('workspace', 'internet_archive_saducismus_search.json')
with open(results_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
json.dump(archive_results, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)

print(f'\nüíæ INTERNET ARCHIVE RESULTS SAVED TO: {results_file}')

# Analysis summary
archive_results['analysis'] = {
'total_searches': len(archive_results['searches']),
'documents_found': len(archive_results['documents_found']),
'suffolk_references': len(archive_results['suffolk_references']),
'success_rate': len(archive_results['documents_found']) > 0
}

print('\nüìä INTERNET ARCHIVE SEARCH SUMMARY:')
print(f' ‚Ä¢ Searches conducted: {archive_results["analysis"]["total_searches"]}')
print(f' ‚Ä¢ Relevant documents found: {archive_results["analysis"]["documents_found"]}')
print(f' ‚Ä¢ Suffolk references extracted: {archive_results["analysis"]["suffolk_references"]}')
print(f' ‚Ä¢ Search successful: {archive_results["analysis"]["success_rate"]}')

print('\nüéØ NEXT STEPS:')
if archive_results['suffolk_references']:
print('‚úÖ Suffolk references found - proceed to identify specific locations')
print('‚úÖ Then research artists/suffragettes from those Suffolk places')
elif archive_results['documents_found']:
print('‚ö†Ô∏è Documents found but no Suffolk references yet')
print('üîç Need to examine full text content more thoroughly')
print('üîç Or search for additional 17th century supernatural compilations')
else:
print('‚ùå No relevant documents found in Internet Archive')
print('üîÑ Try alternative approaches:')
print(' ‚Ä¢ Project Gutenberg for digitized historical texts')
print(' ‚Ä¢ HathiTrust Digital Library')
print(' ‚Ä¢ Google Books (different approach than web search)')
print(' ‚Ä¢ Academic databases with historical collections')

print('\n=== INTERNET ARCHIVE SEARCH PHASE COMPLETE ===')

### Development Step 54: Identify 17th-Century Spectral Army Records, Locate Suffolk Supernatural Sites, Research Artist-Suffragette Locals

**Description**: Search for historical documents from the 17th century that record both a spectral army apparition in Ireland and supernatural events in Britain, focusing on identifying works like Joseph Glanvill's 'Saducismus Triumphatus' (1681) or similar collections of supernatural accounts. These compilations often documented multiple paranormal events across different locations. Once the specific document is identified, locate any Suffolk locations mentioned in connection with unusual supernatural events, then research notable individuals from that actual Suffolk place who were both artists and suffragettes.

**Use Cases**:
- Curatorial research for a Suffolk museum to identify 17th-century artist-suffragette figures from digitized archives and plan a themed exhibition
- Genealogy firm automating extraction from parish HTML and JSON records to help clients trace ancestors active in both art and women‚Äôs suffrage in Suffolk
- Digital humanities project mapping 17th-century paranormal accounts alongside local biographical data to build an interactive web atlas of supernatural events and notable residents
- University history department processing research files to cross-reference Glanvill‚Äôs ‚ÄòSaducismus Triumphatus‚Äô references with Suffolk artist-activists for a peer-reviewed journal article
- Cultural heritage NGO compiling an online database of female artist-suffragettes in rural Suffolk by scraping saved HTML research pages and structured JSON leads
- Local tourism board generating guided tour itineraries highlighting sites linked to prominent Suffolk suffragettes and artists, based on automated text analysis of archival materials
- Educational platform auto-generating lesson modules on East Anglian women‚Äôs history by extracting and validating names from digitized Suffolk research files
- Arts funding body analyzing extracted individual profiles to prioritize grants for preserving suffrage movement art heritage sites in Suffolk

```
import os
import json
from bs4 import BeautifulSoup
import re

print('=== EXTRACTING SPECIFIC ARTIST/SUFFRAGETTE NAMES FROM SUFFOLK RESEARCH FILES ===')
print('Previous search identified 5 promising Suffolk locations with artist/suffragette connections')
print('Now extracting specific individual names from the saved HTML research files\n')

# Ensure workspace directory exists
os.makedirs('workspace', exist_ok=True)

# First, let's inspect the comprehensive research file to understand its structure
research_file = os.path.join('workspace', 'comprehensive_historical_suffolk_research.json')

print('=== PHASE 1: INSPECTING SAVED RESEARCH DATA ===')
print('=' * 70)

if os.path.exists(research_file):
print(f'Found research file: {research_file}')

try:
with open(research_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
research_data = json.load(f)

print('Research file structure:')
for key in research_data.keys():
if isinstance(research_data[key], list):
print(f' ‚Ä¢ {key}: {len(research_data[key])} items')
elif isinstance(research_data[key], dict):
print(f' ‚Ä¢ {key}: {len(research_data[key])} keys')
else:
print(f' ‚Ä¢ {key}: {type(research_data[key]).__name__}')

# Examine the artist_suffragette_leads structure
if 'artist_suffragette_leads' in research_data:
print(f'\nArtist/Suffragette leads found: {len(research_data["artist_suffragette_leads"])}')

for i, lead in enumerate(research_data['artist_suffragette_leads'], 1):
print(f' {i}. {lead["location"]} - Promising: {lead.get("promising", False)}')
if 'artist_search' in lead and 'file' in lead['artist_search']:
print(f' Artist file: {lead["artist_search"]["file"]}')
if 'suffragette_search' in lead and 'file' in lead['suffragette_search']:
print(f' Suffragette file: {lead["suffragette_search"]["file"]}')

except Exception as e:
print(f'Error reading research file: {str(e)}')
else:
print(f'Research file not found: {research_file}')
print('Checking for alternative research files...')

# Look for any JSON files in workspace
json_files = [f for f in os.listdir('workspace') if f.endswith('.json')]
print(f'Found {len(json_files)} JSON files:')
for f in json_files:
print(f' ‚Ä¢ {f}')

print('\n=== PHASE 2: EXAMINING HTML RESEARCH FILES FOR SPECIFIC NAMES ===')
print('=' * 80)

# Look for HTML files related to Suffolk locations
html_files = [f for f in os.listdir('workspace') if f.endswith('.html') and any(location in f.lower() for location in ['aldeburgh', 'bury', 'lavenham', 'melford', 'woodbridge'])]

print(f'Found {len(html_files)} Suffolk location HTML files:')
for f in html_files:
print(f' ‚Ä¢ {f}')

# Initialize results storage
name_extraction_results = {
'timestamp': '2024-12-19',
'objective': 'Extract specific artist and suffragette names from Suffolk location research',
'locations_analyzed': [],
'individuals_found': [],
'analysis_summary': {}
}

# Process each HTML file to extract names
for html_file in html_files:
print(f'\n--- Analyzing {html_file} ---')

# Determine location from filename
location = 'Unknown'
if 'aldeburgh' in html_file.lower():
location = 'Aldeburgh'
elif 'bury' in html_file.lower():
location = 'Bury St Edmunds'
elif 'lavenham' in html_file.lower():
location = 'Lavenham'
elif 'melford' in html_file.lower():
location = 'Long Melford'
elif 'woodbridge' in html_file.lower():
location = 'Woodbridge'

# Determine if this is artist or suffragette search
search_type = 'artist' if 'artist' in html_file.lower() else 'suffragette'

print(f'Location: {location}, Search type: {search_type}')

try:
html_filepath = os.path.join('workspace', html_file)
with open(html_filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
html_content = f.read()

print(f'File size: {len(html_content):,} characters')

# Parse HTML content
soup = BeautifulSoup(html_content, 'html.parser')

# Extract text content
page_text = soup.get_text()

# Look for potential names using various patterns
potential_names = set()

# Pattern 1: Names in titles or headings
for heading in soup.find_all(['h1', 'h2', 'h3', 'h4', 'title']):
heading_text = heading.get_text().strip()
# Look for capitalized words that might be names
name_matches = re.findall(r'\b[A-Z][a-z]+ [A-Z][a-z]+\b', heading_text)
potential_names.update(name_matches)

# Pattern 2: Names in context with artist/suffragette keywords
text_lines = page_text.split('\n')
for line in text_lines:
line = line.strip()
if len(line) > 20 and len(line) < 200: # Reasonable line length
# Look for lines containing relevant keywords
if search_type == 'artist':
if any(keyword in line.lower() for keyword in ['artist', 'painter', 'sculptor', 'born', 'lived']):
name_matches = re.findall(r'\b[A-Z][a-z]+ [A-Z][a-z]+\b', line)
potential_names.update(name_matches)
else: # suffragette
if any(keyword in line.lower() for keyword in ['suffragette', 'suffrage', 'women', 'rights', 'activist']):
name_matches = re.findall(r'\b[A-Z][a-z]+ [A-Z][a-z]+\b', line)
potential_names.update(name_matches)

# Pattern 3: Names in link text or descriptions
for link in soup.find_all('a'):
link_text = link.get_text().strip()
if len(link_text) > 5 and len(link_text) < 100:
name_matches = re.findall(r'\b[A-Z][a-z]+ [A-Z][a-z]+\b', link_text)
potential_names.update(name_matches)

# Filter out common false positives
filtered_names = set()
false_positives = {'New York', 'United States', 'Great Britain', 'Long Island', 'New England',
'World War', 'First World', 'Second World', 'High School', 'Art Gallery',
'Art Museum', 'Women Rights', 'Human Rights', 'Civil Rights', 'Royal Academy'}

for name in potential_names:
if name not in false_positives and len(name.split()) == 2:
# Additional filtering for likely person names
first_name, last_name = name.split()
if len(first_name) > 2 and len(last_name) > 2:
filtered_names.add(name)

print(f'Found {len(filtered_names)} potential names: {list(filtered_names)[:5]}...')

# Store results
location_analysis = {
'location': location,
'search_type': search_type,
'html_file': html_file,
'potential_names': list(filtered_names),
'name_count': len(filtered_names)
}

name_extraction_results['locations_analyzed'].append(location_analysis)

# Add individual names to master list
for name in filtered_names:
individual_entry = {
'name': name,
'location': location,
'type': search_type,
'source_file': html_file
}
name_extraction_results['individuals_found'].append(individual_entry)

# Show most promising findings
if len(filtered_names) > 0:
print(f'üéØ NAMES FOUND in {location} ({search_type}):'):
for name in list(filtered_names)[:3]: # Show top 3
print(f' ‚Ä¢ {name}')
else:
print(f'‚ùå No clear names found in {location} ({search_type})')

except Exception as e:
print(f'Error processing {html_file}: {str(e)}')

print('\n=== PHASE 3: ANALYZING EXTRACTED NAMES AND IDENTIFYING MOST PROMISING CANDIDATES ===')
print('=' * 90)

total_individuals = len(name_extraction_results['individuals_found'])
print(f'Total individuals extracted: {total_individuals}')

if total_individuals > 0:
# Group by location
by_location = {}
by_type = {'artist': [], 'suffragette': []}

for individual in name_extraction_results['individuals_found']:
location = individual['location']
if location not in by_location:
by_location[location] = []
by_location[location].append(individual)

by_type[individual['type']].append(individual)

print(f'\nüìç INDIVIDUALS BY LOCATION:')
for location, individuals in by_location.items():
print(f' {location}: {len(individuals)} individuals')
artists = [i for i in individuals if i['type'] == 'artist']
suffragettes = [i for i in individuals if i['type'] == 'suffragette']
print(f' ‚Ä¢ Artists: {len(artists)}')
print(f' ‚Ä¢ Suffragettes: {len(suffragettes)}')

# Show sample names
if artists:
print(f' ‚Ä¢ Sample artists: {", ".join([a["name"] for a in artists[:2]])}')
if suffragettes:
print(f' ‚Ä¢ Sample suffragettes: {", ".join([s["name"] for s in suffragettes[:2]])}')

print(f'\nüë• INDIVIDUALS BY TYPE:')
print(f' Artists: {len(by_type["artist"])}')
print(f' Suffragettes: {len(by_type["suffragette"])}')

# Identify individuals who appear in both categories (most promising)
artist_names = set([i['name'] for i in by_type['artist']])
suffragette_names = set([i['name'] for i in by_type['suffragette']])

dual_individuals = artist_names.intersection(suffragette_names)

if dual_individuals:
print(f'\nüéØ INDIVIDUALS WHO ARE BOTH ARTISTS AND SUFFRAGETTES ({len(dual_individuals)}):'):
for name in dual_individuals:
# Find their locations
locations = set()
for individual in name_extraction_results['individuals_found']:
if individual['name'] == name:
locations.add(individual['location'])
print(f' ‚Ä¢ {name} (from {', '.join(locations)})')
else:
print('\n‚ùå No individuals found who are both artists and suffragettes')
print('Showing top candidates from each category:')

if by_type['artist']:
print('\nüé® TOP ARTISTS:')
unique_artists = list(set([i['name'] for i in by_type['artist']]))
for name in unique_artists[:5]:
locations = [i['location'] for i in by_type['artist'] if i['name'] == name]
print(f' ‚Ä¢ {name} (from {', '.join(set(locations))})')

if by_type['suffragette']:
print('\nüó≥Ô∏è TOP SUFFRAGETTES:')
unique_suffragettes = list(set([i['name'] for i in by_type['suffragette']]))
for name in unique_suffragettes[:5]:
locations = [i['location'] for i in by_type['suffragette'] if i['name'] == name]
print(f' ‚Ä¢ {name} (from {', '.join(set(locations))})')
else:
print('‚ùå No individual names were successfully extracted from the research files')
print('This could indicate:')
print(' ‚Ä¢ The HTML files may not contain detailed biographical information')
print(' ‚Ä¢ The search results may be too general or not focused on individuals')
print(' ‚Ä¢ Additional targeted searches may be needed for specific people')

# Save extraction results
extraction_file = os.path.join('workspace', 'suffolk_individuals_extracted.json')

name_extraction_results['analysis_summary'] = {
'total_individuals': total_individuals,
'locations_with_findings': len([loc for loc in name_extraction_results['locations_analyzed'] if loc['name_count'] > 0]),
'artists_found': len([i for i in name_extraction_results['individuals_found'] if i['type'] == 'artist']),
'suffragettes_found': len([i for i in name_extraction_results['individuals_found'] if i['type'] == 'suffragette']),
'dual_individuals': len(dual_individuals) if total_individuals > 0 else 0
}

with open(extraction_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
json.dump(name_extraction_results, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)

print(f'\nüíæ NAME EXTRACTION RESULTS SAVED TO: {extraction_file}')

print('\n=== PHASE 4: RECOMMENDATIONS FOR COMPLETING THE RESEARCH ===')
print('=' * 80)

if total_individuals > 0:
print('‚úÖ SUCCESS: Individual names have been extracted from Suffolk location research')
print('\nüéØ NEXT STEPS TO COMPLETE THE RESEARCH:')
print('1. üìö Conduct detailed biographical research on the extracted individuals')
print('2. ‚úÖ Verify their connections to both art and suffrage movements')
print('3. üìç Confirm their association with the identified Suffolk locations')
print('4. üîç Cross-reference with historical records and databases')

if dual_individuals:
print(f'5. üéØ Priority focus on dual individuals: {", ".join(list(dual_individuals)[:3])}')
else:
print('5. üîÑ Research connections between top artists and suffragettes from same locations')
else:
print('‚ö†Ô∏è ALTERNATIVE APPROACH NEEDED:')
print('1. üîç Conduct more targeted searches for specific Suffolk artists')
print('2. üìö Search historical databases and archives directly')
print('3. üèõÔ∏è Check local Suffolk historical society records')
print('4. üìñ Examine biographical dictionaries of British artists and suffragettes')

print('\nüìä FINAL EXTRACTION STATISTICS:')
for key, value in name_extraction_results['analysis_summary'].items():
print(f' ‚Ä¢ {key.replace("_", " ").title()}: {value}')

print('\n=== SUFFOLK ARTIST/SUFFRAGETTE NAME EXTRACTION COMPLETE ===')

import os import requests from bs4 import BeautifulSoup import json import time from urllib.parse import quote_plus print('=== COMPREHENSIVE SEARCH FOR SARASOTA THEATER COMPANY ===') print('Objective: Find theater company with 18th-century Italian theater, rotating repertory, and London Study Program') print('Target: Recent productions of 15th-century plays\n') # Ensure workspace directory exists os.makedirs('workspace', exist_ok=True) # Initialize search results storage search_results = { 'timestamp': time.strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'), 'objective': 'Find Sarasota theater company with specific criteria', 'search_queries': [], 'companies_found': [], 'productions_found': [], 'analysis': {} } # Get SerpAPI key from environment variables api_key = os.getenv("SERPAPI_API_KEY") if api_key is None: print("Error: Missing API key. Make sure you have SERPAPI_API_KEY in your environment variables.") else: print("‚úÖ SerpAPI key found - proceeding with searches\n") # Define comprehensive search queries search_queries = [ "Sarasota 18th century Italian theater reassembled", "Sarasota theater company rotating repertory system", "Sarasota conservatory London Study Program Shakespeare", "Italian theater Sarasota Florida historic venue", "Sarasota Shakespeare theater company conservatory", "18th century theater building Sarasota repertory", "Sarasota theater London program Shakespearean techniques", "historic Italian theater reassembled Florida Sarasota" ] print('=== PHASE 1: CONDUCTING TARGETED WEB SEARCHES ===') print('=' * 70) for i, query in enumerate(search_queries, 1): print(f'\nSearch {i}: {query}') print('-' * 50) try: # Prepare API request parameters params = { "q": query, "api_key": api_key, "engine": "google", "google_domain": "google.com", "safe": "off", "num": 10, "type": "search" } # Make API request to SerpAPI response = requests.get("https://serpapi.com/search.json", params=params) if response.status_code == 200: results = response.json() if results.get("organic_results"): print(f'Found {len(results["organic_results"])} results') # Process and analyze results relevant_results = [] for j, result in enumerate(results["organic_results"], 1): title = result.get('title', 'No title') snippet = result.get('snippet', 'No snippet') link = result.get('link', 'No link') # Check relevance based on keywords combined_text = f'{title} {snippet}'.lower() relevance_indicators = [] if 'sarasota' in combined_text: relevance_indicators.append('sarasota') if 'italian' in combined_text: relevance_indicators.append('italian') if 'theater' in combined_text or 'theatre' in combined_text: relevance_indicators.append('theater') if '18th century' in combined_text or 'eighteenth century' in combined_text: relevance_indicators.append('18th-century') if 'repertory' in combined_text: relevance_indicators.append('repertory') if 'conservatory' in combined_text: relevance_indicators.append('conservatory') if 'london' in combined_text: relevance_indicators.append('london') if 'shakespeare' in combined_text: relevance_indicators.append('shakespeare') if 'reassembled' in combined_text or 'reconstructed' in combined_text: relevance_indicators.append('reassembled') if len(relevance_indicators) >= 2: # At least 2 relevant terms print(f' {j}. {title[:80]}...') print(f' Relevance: {', '.join(relevance_indicators)}') print(f' Link: {link}') print(f' Snippet: {snippet[:100]}...') relevant_results.append({ 'title': title, 'snippet': snippet, 'link': link, 'relevance_terms': relevance_indicators, 'query': query }) # Store search results search_results['search_queries'].append({ 'query': query, 'results_count': len(results["organic_results"]), 'relevant_results': relevant_results }) # If we found highly relevant results, mark potential companies high_relevance = [r for r in relevant_results if len(r['relevance_terms']) >= 3] if high_relevance: print(f'\nüéØ HIGH RELEVANCE RESULTS: {len(high_relevance)}') for result in high_relevance: # Check if this looks like a theater company combined = f'{result["title"]} {result["snippet"]}'.lower() company_indicators = ['company', 'theatre', 'theater', 'opera', 'conservatory', 'academy'] if any(indicator in combined for indicator in company_indicators): search_results['companies_found'].append(result) print(f' üèõÔ∏è POTENTIAL COMPANY: {result["title"]}') else: print(f'No results found for "{query}"') else: print(f'API request failed with status {response.status_code}: {response.text}') # Rate limiting time.sleep(1) except Exception as e: print(f'Error with search "{query}": {str(e)}') continue print('\n' + '=' * 80) print('PHASE 2: ANALYZING SEARCH RESULTS FOR THEATER COMPANIES') print('=' * 80) total_companies = len(search_results['companies_found']) print(f'Total potential companies identified: {total_companies}') if total_companies > 0: print('\nüèõÔ∏è POTENTIAL THEATER COMPANIES FOUND:') print('-' * 50) # Remove duplicates based on similar titles or domains unique_companies = [] seen_domains = set() for company in search_results['companies_found']: # Extract domain from link try: from urllib.parse import urlparse domain = urlparse(company['link']).netloc.lower() if domain not in seen_domains: seen_domains.add(domain) unique_companies.append(company) except: unique_companies.append(company) print(f'Unique companies after deduplication: {len(unique_companies)}') # Sort by relevance (number of matching terms) unique_companies.sort(key=lambda x: len(x['relevance_terms']), reverse=True) for i, company in enumerate(unique_companies, 1): print(f'\n{i}. {company["title"]}') print(f' Relevance terms: {', '.join(company["relevance_terms"])}') print(f' From query: {company["query"]}') print(f' Link: {company["link"]}') print(f' Description: {company["snippet"][:150]}...') # If this company has very high relevance, try to get more details if len(company['relevance_terms']) >= 4: print(f' üéØ EXTREMELY RELEVANT - Will investigate further') # Save companies for further investigation companies_file = os.path.join('workspace', 'sarasota_theater_companies.json') with open(companies_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(unique_companies, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False) print(f'\nüíæ Company data saved to: {companies_file}') else: print('‚ùå No theater companies clearly identified from search results') print('This may indicate need for more specific search terms or different approach') print('\n=== PHASE 3: SEARCHING FOR 15TH-CENTURY PLAY PRODUCTIONS ===') print('=' * 80) # Now search specifically for 15th-century plays in Sarasota production_queries = [ "Sarasota theater 15th century plays productions", "Sarasota repertory 15th century medieval drama", "Sarasota Shakespeare 15th century Renaissance plays", "15th century plays performed Sarasota Florida theater", "medieval drama Sarasota theater company recent productions" ] for i, query in enumerate(production_queries, 1): print(f'\nProduction Search {i}: {query}') print('-' * 50) try: params = { "q": query, "api_key": api_key, "engine": "google", "google_domain": "google.com", "safe": "off", "num": 10, "type": "search" } response = requests.get("https://serpapi.com/search.json", params=params) if response.status_code == 200: results = response.json() if results.get("organic_results"): print(f'Found {len(results["organic_results"])} results') for j, result in enumerate(results["organic_results"], 1): title = result.get('title', 'No title') snippet = result.get('snippet', 'No snippet') link = result.get('link', 'No link') combined_text = f'{title} {snippet}'.lower() # Look for specific 15th-century play titles or production mentions production_indicators = [] if '15th century' in combined_text or 'fifteenth century' in combined_text: production_indicators.append('15th-century') if 'medieval' in combined_text: production_indicators.append('medieval') if 'production' in combined_text or 'performance' in combined_text: production_indicators.append('production') if 'season' in combined_text or 'repertory' in combined_text: production_indicators.append('season') if any(year in combined_text for year in ['2023', '2024', '2022']): production_indicators.append('recent') # Look for specific play titles (common 15th-century works) play_titles = ['everyman', 'mankind', 'morality play', 'mystery play', 'passion play'] found_plays = [play for play in play_titles if play in combined_text] if production_indicators or found_plays: print(f' {j}. {title[:80]}...') if production_indicators: print(f' Production indicators: {', '.join(production_indicators)}') if found_plays: print(f' üé≠ Potential plays: {', '.join(found_plays)}') print(f' Link: {link}') print(f' Snippet: {snippet[:120]}...') search_results['productions_found'].append({ 'title': title, 'snippet': snippet, 'link': link, 'production_indicators': production_indicators, 'potential_plays': found_plays, 'query': query }) else: print(f'No results found for "{query}"') time.sleep(1) except Exception as e: print(f'Error with production search "{query}": {str(e)}') continue # Save all search results results_file = os.path.join('workspace', 'sarasota_theater_comprehensive_search.json') with open(results_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(search_results, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False) print(f'\nüíæ COMPREHENSIVE SEARCH RESULTS SAVED TO: {results_file}') # Analysis summary search_results['analysis'] = { 'total_searches': len(search_results['search_queries']) + len(production_queries), 'companies_identified': len(search_results['companies_found']), 'productions_found': len(search_results['productions_found']), 'success_indicators': [] } if search_results['companies_found']: search_results['analysis']['success_indicators'].append('Theater companies identified') if search_results['productions_found']: search_results['analysis']['success_indicators'].append('Productions found') print('\nüìä COMPREHENSIVE SEARCH SUMMARY:') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Total searches conducted: {search_results["analysis"]["total_searches"]}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Theater companies identified: {search_results["analysis"]["companies_identified"]}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Productions found: {search_results["analysis"]["productions_found"]}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Success indicators: {", ".join(search_results["analysis"]["success_indicators"]) if search_results["analysis"]["success_indicators"] else "None"}') print('\nüéØ NEXT STEPS:') if search_results['companies_found']: print('‚úÖ Theater companies identified - proceed to detailed investigation') print('‚úÖ Access company websites for production schedules and program details') if search_results['productions_found']: print('‚úÖ Production references found - analyze for specific 15th-century play titles') else: print('‚ö†Ô∏è Limited production information found - may need targeted website searches') print('\n=== SARASOTA THEATER COMPANY SEARCH COMPLETE ===')

Look for specific 15th-century play titles or production mentions production_indicators = [] if '15th century' in combined_text or 'fifteenth century' in combined_text: production_indicators.append('15th-century') if 'medieval' in combined_text: production_indicators.append('medieval') if 'production' in combined_text or 'performance' in combined_text: production_indicators.append('production') if 'season' in combined_text or 'repertory' in combined_text: production_indicators.append('season') if any(year in combined_text for year in ['2023', '2024', '2022']): production_indicators.append('recent') # Look for specific play titles (common 15th-century works) play_titles = ['everyman', 'mankind', 'morality play', 'mystery play', 'passion play'] found_plays = [play for play in play_titles if play in combined_text] if production_indicators or found_plays: print(f' {j}. {title[:80]}...') if production_indicators: print(f' Production indicators: {', '.join(production_indicators)}') if found_plays: print(f' üé≠ Potential plays: {', '.join(found_plays)}') print(f' Link: {link}') print(f' Snippet: {snippet[:120]}...') search_results['productions_found'].append({ 'title': title, 'snippet': snippet, 'link': link, 'production_indicators': production_indicators, 'potential_plays': found_plays, 'query': query }) else: print(f'No results found for "{query}"') time.sleep(1) except Exception as e: print(f'Error with production search "{query}": {str(e)}') continue # Save all search results results_file = os.path.join('workspace', 'sarasota_theater_comprehensive_search.json') with open(results_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(search_results, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False) print(f'\nüíæ COMPREHENSIVE SEARCH RESULTS SAVED TO: {results_file}') # Analysis summary search_results['analysis'] = { 'total_searches': len(search_results['search_queries']) + len(production_queries), 'companies_identified': len(search_results['companies_found']), 'productions_found': len(search_results['productions_found']), 'success_indicators': [] } if search_results['companies_found']: search_results['analysis']['success_indicators'].append('Theater companies identified') if search_results['productions_found']: search_results['analysis']['success_indicators'].append('Productions found') print('\nüìä COMPREHENSIVE SEARCH SUMMARY:') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Total searches conducted: {search_results["analysis"]["total_searches"]}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Theater companies identified: {search_results["analysis"]["companies_identified"]}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Productions found: {search_results["analysis"]["productions_found"]}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Success indicators: {", ".join(search_results["analysis"]["success_indicators"]) if search_results["analysis"]["success_indicators"] else "None"}') print('\nüéØ NEXT STEPS:') if search_results['companies_found']: print('‚úÖ Theater companies identified - proceed to detailed investigation') print('‚úÖ Access company websites for production schedules and program details') if search_results['productions_found']: print('‚úÖ Production references found - analyze for specific 15th-century play titles') else: print('‚ö†Ô∏è Limited production information found - may need targeted website searches') print('\n=== SARASOTA THEATER COMPANY SEARCH COMPLETE ===')

import os import requests from bs4 import BeautifulSoup import json import time from urllib.parse import urljoin, urlparse print('=== DIRECT WEB SCRAPING FOR SARASOTA THEATER COMPANIES ===') print('Switching to direct web scraping approach due to API quota exhaustion') print('Target: Theater company with 18th-century Italian theater, rotating repertory, London Study Program\n') # Ensure workspace directory exists os.makedirs('workspace', exist_ok=True) # Initialize results storage scraping_results = { 'timestamp': time.strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'), 'method': 'Direct web scraping', 'objective': 'Find Sarasota theater company with specific criteria', 'websites_scraped': [], 'companies_found': [], 'productions_found': [], 'analysis': {} } # Headers for web requests headers = { 'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/91.0.4472.124 Safari/537.36', 'Accept': 'text/html,application/xhtml+xml,application/xml;q=0.9,*/*;q=0.8', 'Accept-Language': 'en-US,en;q=0.5', 'Accept-Encoding': 'gzip, deflate', 'Connection': 'keep-alive' } print('=== PHASE 1: IDENTIFYING SARASOTA THEATER ORGANIZATIONS ===') print('=' * 70) # Request the main page response = requests.get(site_info['url'], headers=headers, timeout=15) print(f'Status: {response.status_code}') if response.status_code == 200: # Save the page filename = f'{site_info["name"].lower().replace(" ", "_")}_homepage.html' filepath = os.path.join('workspace', filename) with open(filepath, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: f.write(response.text) print(f'Saved: {filepath}') # Parse the content soup = BeautifulSoup(response.text, 'html.parser') page_text = soup.get_text().lower() # Check for key criteria criteria_matches = { '18th_century_italian': False, 'rotating_repertory': False, 'london_study_program': False, 'conservatory': False, 'shakespeare': False, 'italian_theater': False, 'reassembled': False } # Search for 18th century Italian theater indicators if any(term in page_text for term in ['18th century', 'eighteenth century', 'italian theater', 'italian theatre', 'historic theater', 'historic theatre']): criteria_matches['18th_century_italian'] = True print(' ‚úÖ Found 18th century/Italian theater references') # Search for repertory system indicators if any(term in page_text for term in ['repertory', 'rotating', 'season', 'multiple productions']): criteria_matches['rotating_repertory'] = True print(' ‚úÖ Found repertory system references') # Search for London Study Program indicators if any(term in page_text for term in ['london', 'study abroad', 'international program', 'study program']): criteria_matches['london_study_program'] = True print(' ‚úÖ Found London/study program references') # Search for conservatory indicators if any(term in page_text for term in ['conservatory', 'training program', 'mfa', 'graduate program']): criteria_matches['conservatory'] = True print(' ‚úÖ Found conservatory references') # Search for Shakespeare indicators if 'shakespeare' in page_text: criteria_matches['shakespeare'] = True print(' ‚úÖ Found Shakespeare references') # Search for Italian theater indicators if any(term in page_text for term in ['italian', 'historic theater', 'reassembled', 'reconstructed']): criteria_matches['italian_theater'] = True print(' ‚úÖ Found Italian/historic theater references') # Calculate match score match_score = sum(criteria_matches.values()) print(f' üìä Criteria match score: {match_score}/7') # Store results site_analysis = { 'name': site_info['name'], 'url': site_info['url'], 'status_code': response.status_code, 'criteria_matches': criteria_matches, 'match_score': match_score, 'html_file': filepath, 'page_length': len(response.text) } scraping_results['websites_scraped'].append(site_analysis) # If high match score, mark as potential company if match_score >= 3: print(f' üéØ HIGH POTENTIAL COMPANY (Score: {match_score})') scraping_results['companies_found'].append(site_analysis) # Try to find more specific information print(' üîç Looking for additional details...') # Look for about/history pages about_links = [] for link in soup.find_all('a', href=True): link_text = link.get_text().lower() href = link.get('href') if any(keyword in link_text for keyword in ['about', 'history', 'theater', 'venue', 'facility', 'conservatory', 'program']): full_url = urljoin(site_info['url'], href) about_links.append({ 'text': link_text.strip(), 'url': full_url }) print(f' Found {len(about_links)} relevant internal links') for link in about_links[:3]: # Show first 3 print(f' - {link["text"]}: {link["url"]}') # Try to access the most promising about page if about_links: most_relevant = about_links[0] print(f' üîç Accessing: {most_relevant["text"]}...') try: about_response = requests.get(most_relevant['url'], headers=headers, timeout=10) if about_response.status_code == 200: about_filename = f'{site_info["name"].lower().replace(" ", "_")}_about.html' about_filepath = os.path.join('workspace', about_filename) with open(about_filepath, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: f.write(about_response.text) print(f' ‚úÖ Saved about page: {about_filename}') # Quick analysis of about page about_soup = BeautifulSoup(about_response.text, 'html.parser') about_text = about_soup.get_text().lower() # Look for specific details if 'asolo' in about_text and 'italian' in about_text: print(' üéØ FOUND ASOLO ITALIAN THEATER REFERENCE!') if 'fsu' in about_text or 'florida state' in about_text: print(' üéØ FOUND FSU CONNECTION!') if 'london' in about_text: print(' üéØ FOUND LONDON PROGRAM REFERENCE!') except Exception as e: print(f' ‚ùå Error accessing about page: {str(e)}') else: print(f' ‚ùå Low match score ({match_score}) - not a strong candidate') else: print(f' ‚ùå Failed to access website (Status: {response.status_code})') except Exception as e: print(f' ‚ùå Error scraping {site_info["name"]}: {str(e)}') # Rate limiting time.sleep(2) print('\n=== PHASE 3: ANALYZING RESULTS AND IDENTIFYING TOP CANDIDATES ===') print('=' * 80) total_scraped = len(scraping_results['websites_scraped']) total_companies = len(scraping_results['companies_found']) print(f'Websites successfully scraped: {total_scraped}') print(f'High-potential companies identified: {total_companies}') if total_companies > 0: print('\nüèõÔ∏è TOP CANDIDATE COMPANIES:') print('-' * 50) # Sort by match score scraping_results['companies_found'].sort(key=lambda x: x['match_score'], reverse=True) for i, company in enumerate(scraping_results['companies_found'], 1): print(f'\n{i}. {company["name"]} (Score: {company["match_score"]}/7)') print(f' URL: {company["url"]}') print(f' Criteria matches:') for criterion, matched in company['criteria_matches'].items(): status = '‚úÖ' if matched else '‚ùå' criterion_display = criterion.replace('_', ' ').title() print(f' {status} {criterion_display}') print(f' Saved data: {company["html_file"]}') # If this is the top candidate, provide detailed analysis if i == 1: print('\n üéØ TOP CANDIDATE ANALYSIS:') if company['match_score'] >= 5: print(' ‚≠ê EXCELLENT MATCH - Very likely to be the target company') elif company['match_score'] >= 3: print(' ‚≠ê GOOD MATCH - Strong candidate, needs verification') else: print(' ‚ö†Ô∏è MODERATE MATCH - May need additional investigation') else: print('\n‚ùå No high-potential companies identified from initial scraping') print('This may indicate:') print(' ‚Ä¢ Need to search additional Sarasota theater organizations') print(' ‚Ä¢ Criteria may be on secondary pages not captured') print(' ‚Ä¢ Target company may have different online presence') print('\n=== PHASE 4: SEARCHING FOR 15TH-CENTURY PLAY PRODUCTIONS ===') print('=' * 80) # For companies found, try to find production information if scraping_results['companies_found']: top_company = scraping_results['companies_found'][0] print(f'Searching for productions at top candidate: {top_company["name"]}') try: # Look for season/productions pages base_url = top_company['url'] production_urls = [ f'{base_url}/season', f'{base_url}/productions', f'{base_url}/current-season', f'{base_url}/shows', f'{base_url}/calendar' ] for prod_url in production_urls: print(f'\nTrying: {prod_url}') try: prod_response = requests.get(prod_url, headers=headers, timeout=10) if prod_response.status_code == 200: print(f' ‚úÖ Found productions page!') # Save productions page prod_filename = f'{top_company["name"].lower().replace(" ", "_")}_productions.html' prod_filepath = os.path.join('workspace', prod_filename) with open(prod_filepath, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: f.write(prod_response.text) print(f' üíæ Saved: {prod_filename}') # Analyze for 15th-century plays prod_soup = BeautifulSoup(prod_response.text, 'html.parser') prod_text = prod_soup.get_text().lower() # Look for 15th-century play indicators century_indicators = ['15th century', 'fifteenth century', 'medieval', '1400s'] play_titles = ['everyman', 'mankind', 'morality play', 'mystery play', 'passion play'] found_indicators = [ind for ind in century_indicators if ind in prod_text] found_plays = [play for play in play_titles if play in prod_text] if found_indicators or found_plays: print(f' üé≠ FOUND 15TH-CENTURY CONTENT!') if found_indicators: print(f' Century indicators: {found_indicators}') if found_plays: print(f' Potential plays: {found_plays}') scraping_results['productions_found'].append({ 'company': top_company['name'], 'url': prod_url, 'century_indicators': found_indicators, 'potential_plays': found_plays, 'file': prod_filepath }) break # Headers for web requests headers = { 'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/91.0.4472.124 Safari/537.36', 'Accept': 'text/html,application/xhtml+xml,application/xml;q=0.9,*/*;q=0.8', 'Accept-Language': 'en-US,en;q=0.5', 'Accept-Encoding': 'gzip, deflate', 'Connection': 'keep-alive' } print('=== PHASE 1: IDENTIFYING SARASOTA THEATER ORGANIZATIONS ===') print('=' * 70) # Known Sarasota theater organizations to investigate target_websites = [ { 'name': 'Sarasota Opera', 'url': 'https://www.sarasotaopera.org', 'rationale': 'Major Sarasota performing arts organization, may have historic theater' }, { 'name': 'Asolo Repertory Theatre', 'url': 'https://www.asolorep.org', 'rationale': 'Repertory theater in Sarasota, likely candidate for rotating repertory system' }, { 'name': 'Florida Studio Theatre', 'url': 'https://www.floridastudiotheatre.org', 'rationale': 'Professional theater company in Sarasota' }, { 'name': 'Sarasota Ballet', 'url': 'https://www.sarasotaballet.org', 'rationale': 'Performing arts organization, may share venues or have theater connections' }, { 'name': 'Ringling College', 'url': 'https://www.ringling.edu', 'rationale': 'Arts college in Sarasota, may have theater program with conservatory elements' }, { 'name': 'FSU/Asolo Conservatory', 'url': 'https://www.asolo.fsu.edu', 'rationale': 'Theater conservatory program, likely candidate for London Study Program' } ] print(f'Investigating {len(target_websites)} potential theater organizations:') for i, site in enumerate(target_websites, 1): print(f' {i}. {site["name"]} - {site["rationale"]}') print('\n=== PHASE 2: SCRAPING THEATER WEBSITES FOR CRITERIA MATCHES ===') print('=' * 80) for i, site_info in enumerate(target_websites, 1): print(f'\n--- Scraping {i}: {site_info["name"]} ---') print(f'URL: {site_info["url"]}') try: # Request the main page response = requests.get(site_info['url'], headers=headers, timeout=15) print(f'Status: {response.status_code}') if response.status_code == 200: # Save the page filename = f'{site_info["name"].lower().replace(" ", "_")}_homepage.html' filepath = os.path.join('workspace', filename) with open(filepath, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: f.write(response.text) print(f'Saved: {filepath}') # Parse the content soup = BeautifulSoup(response.text, 'html.parser') page_text = soup.get_text().lower() # Check for key criteria criteria_matches = { '18th_century_italian': False, 'rotating_repertory': False, 'london_study_program': False, 'conservatory': False, 'shakespeare': False, 'italian_theater': False, 'reassembled': False } # Search for 18th century Italian theater indicators if any(term in page_text for term in ['18th century', 'eighteenth century', 'italian theater', 'italian theatre', 'historic theater', 'historic theatre']): criteria_matches['18th_century_italian'] = True print(' ‚úÖ Found 18th century/Italian theater references') # Search for repertory system indicators if any(term in page_text for term in ['repertory', 'rotating', 'season', 'multiple productions']): criteria_matches['rotating_repertory'] = True print(' ‚úÖ Found repertory system references') # Search for London Study Program indicators if any(term in page_text for term in ['london', 'study abroad', 'international program', 'study program']): criteria_matches['london_study_program'] = True print(' ‚úÖ Found London/study program references') # Search for conservatory indicators if any(term in page_text for term in ['conservatory', 'training program', 'mfa', 'graduate program']): criteria_matches['conservatory'] = True print(' ‚úÖ Found conservatory references') # Search for Shakespeare indicators if 'shakespeare' in page_text: criteria_matches['shakespeare'] = True print(' ‚úÖ Found Shakespeare references') # Search for Italian theater indicators if any(term in page_text for term in ['italian', 'historic theater', 'reassembled', 'reconstructed']): criteria_matches['italian_theater'] = True print(' ‚úÖ Found Italian/historic theater references') # Calculate match score match_score = sum(criteria_matches.values()) print(f' üìä Criteria match score: {match_score}/7') # Store results site_analysis = { 'name': site_info['name'], 'url': site_info['url'], 'status_code': response.status_code, 'criteria_matches': criteria_matches, 'match_score': match_score, 'html_file': filepath, 'page_length': len(response.text) } scraping_results['websites_scraped'].append(site_analysis) # If high match score, mark as potential company if match_score >= 3: print(f' üéØ HIGH POTENTIAL COMPANY (Score: {match_score})') scraping_results['companies_found'].append(site_analysis) # Try to find more specific information print(' üîç Looking for additional details...') # Look for about/history pages about_links = [] for link in soup.find_all('a', href=True): link_text = link.get_text().lower() href = link.get('href') if any(keyword in link_text for keyword in ['about', 'history', 'theater', 'venue', 'facility', 'conservatory', 'program']): full_url = urljoin(site_info['url'], href) about_links.append({ 'text': link_text.strip(), 'url': full_url }) print(f' Found {len(about_links)} relevant internal links') for link in about_links[:3]: # Show first 3 print(f' - {link["text"]}: {link["url"]}') # Try to access the most promising about page if about_links: most_relevant = about_links[0] print(f' üîç Accessing: {most_relevant["text"]}...') try: about_response = requests.get(most_relevant['url'], headers=headers, timeout=10) if about_response.status_code == 200: about_filename = f'{site_info["name"].lower().replace(" ", "_")}_about.html' about_filepath = os.path.join('workspace', about_filename) with open(about_filepath, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: f.write(about_response.text) print(f' ‚úÖ Saved about page: {about_filename}') # Quick analysis of about page about_soup = BeautifulSoup(about_response.text, 'html.parser') about_text = about_soup.get_text().lower() # Look for specific details if 'asolo' in about_text and 'italian' in about_text: print(' üéØ FOUND ASOLO ITALIAN THEATER REFERENCE!') if 'fsu' in about_text or 'florida state' in about_text: print(' üéØ FOUND FSU CONNECTION!') if 'london' in about_text: print(' üéØ FOUND LONDON PROGRAM REFERENCE!') except Exception as e: print(f' ‚ùå Error accessing about page: {str(e)}') else: print(f' ‚ùå Low match score ({match_score}) - not a strong candidate') else: print(f' ‚ùå Failed to access website (Status: {response.status_code})') except Exception as e: print(f' ‚ùå Error scraping {site_info["name"]}: {str(e)}') # Rate limiting time.sleep(2) print('\n=== PHASE 3: ANALYZING RESULTS AND IDENTIFYING TOP CANDIDATES ===') print('=' * 80) total_scraped = len(scraping_results['websites_scraped']) total_companies = len(scraping_results['companies_found']) print(f'Websites successfully scraped: {total_scraped}') print(f'High-potential companies identified: {total_companies}') if total_companies > 0: print('\nüèõÔ∏è TOP CANDIDATE COMPANIES:') print('-' * 50) # Sort by match score scraping_results['companies_found'].sort(key=lambda x: x['match_score'], reverse=True) for i, company in enumerate(scraping_results['companies_found'], 1): print(f'\n{i}. {company["name"]} (Score: {company["match_score"]}/7)') print(f' URL: {company["url"]}') print(f' Criteria matches:') for criterion, matched in company['criteria_matches'].items(): status = '‚úÖ' if matched else '‚ùå' criterion_display = criterion.replace('_', ' ').title() print(f' {status} {criterion_display}') print(f' Saved data: {company["html_file"]}') # If this is the top candidate, provide detailed analysis if i == 1: print('\n üéØ TOP CANDIDATE ANALYSIS:') if company['match_score'] >= 5: print(' ‚≠ê EXCELLENT MATCH - Very likely to be the target company') elif company['match_score'] >= 3: print(' ‚≠ê GOOD MATCH - Strong candidate, needs verification') else: print(' ‚ö†Ô∏è MODERATE MATCH - May need additional investigation') else: print('\n‚ùå No high-potential companies identified from initial scraping') print('This may indicate:') print(' ‚Ä¢ Need to search additional Sarasota theater organizations') print(' ‚Ä¢ Criteria may be on secondary pages not captured') print(' ‚Ä¢ Target company may have different online presence') print('\n=== PHASE 4: SEARCHING FOR 15TH-CENTURY PLAY PRODUCTIONS ===') print('=' * 80) # For companies found, try to find production information if scraping_results['companies_found']: top_company = scraping_results['companies_found'][0] print(f'Searching for productions at top candidate: {top_company["name"]}') try: # Look for season/productions pages base_url = top_company['url'] production_urls = [ f'{base_url}/season', f'{base_url}/productions', f'{base_url}/current-season', f'{base_url}/shows', f'{base_url}/calendar' ] for prod_url in production_urls: print(f'\nTrying: {prod_url}') try: prod_response = requests.get(prod_url, headers=headers, timeout=10) if prod_response.status_code == 200: print(f' ‚úÖ Found productions page!') # Save productions page prod_filename = f'{top_company["name"].lower().replace(" ", "_")}_productions.html' prod_filepath = os.path.join('workspace', prod_filename) with open(prod_filepath, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: f.write(prod_response.text) print(f' üíæ Saved: {prod_filename}') # Analyze for 15th-century plays prod_soup = BeautifulSoup(prod_response.text, 'html.parser') prod_text = prod_soup.get_text().lower() # Look for 15th-century play indicators century_indicators = ['15th century', 'fifteenth century', 'medieval', '1400s'] play_titles = ['everyman', 'mankind', 'morality play', 'mystery play', 'passion play'] found_indicators = [ind for ind in century_indicators if ind in prod_text] found_plays = [play for play in play_titles if play in prod_text] if found_indicators or found_plays: print(f' üé≠ FOUND 15TH-CENTURY CONTENT!') if found_indicators: print(f' Century indicators: {found_indicators}') if found_plays: print(f' Potential plays: {found_plays}') scraping_results['productions_found'].append({ 'company': top_company['name'], 'url': prod_url, 'century_indicators': found_indicators, 'potential_plays': found_plays, 'file': prod_filepath }) break # Found a working productions page except Exception as e: print(f' ‚ùå Error accessing {prod_url}: {str(e)}') continue except Exception as e: print(f'Error searching for productions: {str(e)}') # Save comprehensive results results_file = os.path.join('workspace', 'sarasota_theater_scraping_results.json') with open(results_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(scraping_results, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False) print(f'\nüíæ SCRAPING RESULTS SAVED TO: {results_file}') # Final analysis scraping_results['analysis'] = { 'websites_scraped': len(scraping_results['websites_scraped']), 'companies_identified': len(scraping_results['companies_found']), 'productions_found': len(scraping_results['productions_found']), 'top_candidate': scraping_results['companies_found'][0]['name'] if scraping_results['companies_found'] else None, 'success_rate': len(scraping_results['companies_found']) > 0 } print('\nüìä SCRAPING SUMMARY:') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Websites scraped: {scraping_results["analysis"]["websites_scraped"]}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Companies identified: {scraping_results["analysis"]["companies_identified"]}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Productions found: {scraping_results["analysis"]["productions_found"]}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Top candidate: {scraping_results["analysis"]["top_candidate"] or "None"}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Success: {scraping_results["analysis"]["success_rate"]}') print('\nüéØ CONCLUSIONS:') if scraping_results['companies_found']: top = scraping_results['companies_found'][0] print(f'‚úÖ IDENTIFIED TOP CANDIDATE: {top["name"]}') print(f'‚úÖ Match score: {top["match_score"]}/7 criteria') print(f'‚úÖ Detailed data saved for further analysis') if scraping_results['productions_found']: print(f'‚úÖ Found 15th-century production references') else: print('‚ö†Ô∏è No 15th-century productions found yet - may need deeper investigation') else: print('‚ùå No clear matches found - may need to expand search to additional organizations') print('\n=== SARASOTA THEATER DIRECT SCRAPING COMPLETE ===')

import os import json from bs4 import BeautifulSoup import time print('=== ANALYZING DOWNLOADED SARASOTA THEATER WEBSITES ===') print('Fixing variable scoping issue and analyzing HTML content for criteria matches') print('Target: Theater company with 18th-century Italian theater, rotating repertory, London Study Program\n') # Ensure workspace directory exists os.makedirs('workspace', exist_ok=True) # First, let's inspect what HTML files were successfully downloaded print('=== PHASE 1: INSPECTING DOWNLOADED HTML FILES ===') print('=' * 70) workspace_files = os.listdir('workspace') html_files = [f for f in workspace_files if f.endswith('.html')] print(f'Found {len(html_files)} HTML files in workspace:') for i, filename in enumerate(html_files, 1): filepath = os.path.join('workspace', filename) file_size = os.path.getsize(filepath) print(f' {i}. {filename} ({file_size:,} bytes)') if not html_files: print('‚ùå No HTML files found - previous scraping may have failed') exit() # Initialize results storage analysis_results = { 'timestamp': time.strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'), 'method': 'HTML content analysis (fixed)', 'objective': 'Analyze downloaded Sarasota theater websites for criteria matches', 'files_analyzed': [], 'companies_found': [], 'detailed_analysis': {} } print('\n=== PHASE 2: ANALYZING HTML CONTENT FOR CRITERIA MATCHES ===') print('=' * 80) # Define the criteria we're looking for criteria_keywords = { '18th_century_italian': [ '18th century', 'eighteenth century', 'italian theater', 'italian theatre', 'historic theater', 'historic theatre', 'asolo theater', 'asolo theatre', 'venetian theater', 'venetian theatre', 'reassembled', 'reconstructed' ], 'rotating_repertory': [ 'repertory', 'rotating', 'season', 'multiple productions', 'rep company', 'rotating cast', 'ensemble', 'resident company' ], 'london_study_program': [ 'london', 'study abroad', 'international program', 'study program', 'london study', 'uk program', 'british program', 'overseas study' ], 'conservatory': [ 'conservatory', 'training program', 'mfa', 'graduate program', 'professional training', 'actor training', 'fsu', 'florida state' ], 'shakespeare': [ 'shakespeare', 'shakespearean', 'bard', 'elizabethan', 'classical training' ], 'historic_venue': [ 'historic', 'historical', 'heritage', 'restored', 'original', 'authentic', 'period theater', 'period theatre' ] } print(f'Analyzing {len(html_files)} HTML files for criteria matches...\n') for i, html_file in enumerate(html_files, 1): print(f'--- Analyzing {i}: {html_file} ---') # Determine organization name from filename org_name = html_file.replace('_homepage.html', '').replace('_', ' ').title() print(f'Organization: {org_name}') try: # Read and parse the HTML file filepath = os.path.join('workspace', html_file) with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: html_content = f.read() print(f'File size: {len(html_content):,} characters') # Parse with BeautifulSoup soup = BeautifulSoup(html_content, 'html.parser') # Extract text content (FIXED: proper variable scoping) page_text = soup.get_text().lower() print(f'Text content: {len(page_text):,} characters') # Initialize criteria tracking criteria_matches = {} detailed_findings = {} # Check each criterion total_score = 0 for criterion, keywords in criteria_keywords.items(): matches = [] for keyword in keywords: if keyword.lower() in page_text: matches.append(keyword) criteria_matches[criterion] = len(matches) > 0 detailed_findings[criterion] = matches if matches: total_score += 1 print(f' ‚úÖ {criterion.replace("_", " ").title()}: {matches[:3]}...' if len(matches) > 3 else f' ‚úÖ {criterion.replace("_", " ").title()}: {matches}') else: print(f' ‚ùå {criterion.replace("_", " ").title()}: No matches') print(f' üìä Total criteria score: {total_score}/{len(criteria_keywords)}') # Look for specific organizational details print(' üîç Additional details:') # Extract title title_elem = soup.find('title') page_title = title_elem.get_text().strip() if title_elem else 'No title found' print(f' Title: {page_title}') # Look for contact/location info if 'sarasota' in page_text: print(' üìç Confirmed Sarasota location') # Look for specific mentions that might indicate this is our target special_indicators = [] if 'asolo' in page_text and 'italian' in page_text: special_indicators.append('Asolo Italian Theater connection') if 'fsu' in page_text or 'florida state' in page_text: special_indicators.append('FSU connection') if 'conservatory' in page_text and 'mfa' in page_text: special_indicators.append('MFA Conservatory program') if 'london' in page_text and ('study' in page_text or 'program' in page_text): special_indicators.append('London study program') if special_indicators: print(' üéØ Special indicators:') for indicator in special_indicators: print(f' ‚Ä¢ {indicator}') # Store analysis results file_analysis = { 'filename': html_file, 'organization': org_name, 'page_title': page_title, 'file_size': len(html_content), 'text_length': len(page_text), 'criteria_matches': criteria_matches, 'detailed_findings': detailed_findings, 'total_score': total_score, 'special_indicators': special_indicators } analysis_results['files_analyzed'].append(file_analysis) # If high score, mark as potential target company if total_score >= 3: print(f' üéØ HIGH POTENTIAL COMPANY (Score: {total_score})') analysis_results['companies_found'].append(file_analysis) elif total_score >= 2: print(f' ‚≠ê MODERATE POTENTIAL (Score: {total_score})') else: print(f' ‚ùå LOW POTENTIAL (Score: {total_score})') print() except Exception as e: print(f' ‚ùå Error analyzing {html_file}: {str(e)}') continue print('=== PHASE 3: RANKING AND IDENTIFYING TOP CANDIDATES ===') print('=' * 80) total_analyzed = len(analysis_results['files_analyzed']) total_companies = len(analysis_results['companies_found']) print(f'Files successfully analyzed: {total_analyzed}') print(f'High-potential companies identified: {total_companies}') if total_companies > 0: print('\nüèõÔ∏è TOP CANDIDATE COMPANIES (sorted by score):') print('-' * 60) # Sort companies by total score analysis_results['companies_found'].sort(key=lambda x: x['total_score'], reverse=True) for i, company in enumerate(analysis_results['companies_found'], 1): print(f'\n{i}. {company["organization"]} (Score: {company["total_score"]}/{len(criteria_keywords)})') print(f' File: {company["filename"]}') print(f' Title: {company["page_title"]}') print(' Criteria matches:') for criterion, matched in company['criteria_matches'].items(): status = '‚úÖ' if matched else '‚ùå' criterion_display = criterion.replace('_', ' ').title() if matched and company['detailed_findings'][criterion]: keywords_found = company['detailed_findings'][criterion][:3] # Show first 3 print(f' {status} {criterion_display}: {keywords_found}') else: print(f' {status} {criterion_display}') if company['special_indicators']: print(' üéØ Special indicators:') for indicator in company['special_indicators']: print(f' ‚Ä¢ {indicator}') # Provide assessment if i == 1: # Top candidate print('\n üìã TOP CANDIDATE ASSESSMENT:') score = company['total_score'] if score >= 5: print(' ‚≠ê‚≠ê‚≠ê EXCELLENT MATCH - Very likely the target company') elif score >= 4: print(' ‚≠ê‚≠ê STRONG MATCH - High confidence this is correct') elif score >= 3: print(' ‚≠ê GOOD MATCH - Promising candidate, needs verification') else: print(' ‚ö†Ô∏è MODERATE MATCH - May need additional investigation') else: print('\n‚ùå No high-potential companies identified') print('\nüìä All analyzed companies:') for analysis in analysis_results['files_analyzed']: print(f' ‚Ä¢ {analysis["organization"]}: {analysis["total_score"]}/{len(criteria_keywords)} criteria') print('\n=== PHASE 4: SEARCHING FOR 15TH-CENTURY PRODUCTIONS ===') print('=' * 80) # Look for production-related content in the HTML files production_keywords = [ '15th century', 'fifteenth century', 'medieval', '1400s', 'everyman', 'mankind', 'morality play', 'mystery play', 'passion play', 'medieval drama', 'early drama', 'renaissance', 'period play' ] productions_found = [] for analysis in analysis_results['files_analyzed']: print(f'\nSearching {analysis["organization"]} for 15th-century productions...') try: filepath = os.path.join('workspace', analysis['filename']) with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: html_content = f.read() soup = BeautifulSoup(html_content, 'html.parser') page_text = soup.get_text().lower() # Search for production keywords found_keywords = [] for keyword in production_keywords: if keyword.lower() in page_text: found_keywords.append(keyword) if found_keywords: print(f' üé≠ FOUND 15TH-CENTURY CONTENT: {found_keywords}') productions_found.append({ 'organization': analysis['organization'], 'keywords_found': found_keywords, 'filename': analysis['filename'] }) else: print(f' ‚ùå No 15th-century production references found') except Exception as e: print(f' ‚ùå Error searching productions: {str(e)}') # Save comprehensive analysis results analysis_results['productions_found'] = productions_found analysis_results['summary'] = { 'files_analyzed': total_analyzed, 'companies_identified': total_companies, 'productions_with_15th_century': len(productions_found), 'top_candidate': analysis_results['companies_found'][0]['organization'] if analysis_results['companies_found'] else None, 'top_score': analysis_results['companies_found'][0]['total_score'] if analysis_results['companies_found'] else 0 } results_file = os.path.join('workspace', 'sarasota_theater_analysis_results.json') with open(results_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(analysis_results, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False) print(f'\nüíæ ANALYSIS RESULTS SAVED TO: {results_file}') print('\nüìä FINAL ANALYSIS SUMMARY:') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Files analyzed: {analysis_results["summary"]["files_analyzed"]}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Companies identified: {analysis_results["summary"]["companies_identified"]}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ 15th-century productions found: {analysis_results["summary"]["productions_with_15th_century"]}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Top candidate: {analysis_results["summary"]["top_candidate"] or "None"}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Top score: {analysis_results["summary"]["top_score"]}/{len(criteria_keywords)}') print('\nüéØ CONCLUSIONS AND NEXT STEPS:') if analysis_results['companies_found']: top_company = analysis_results['companies_found'][0] print(f'‚úÖ IDENTIFIED TOP CANDIDATE: {top_company["organization"]}') print(f'‚úÖ Criteria match score: {top_company["total_score"]}/{len(criteria_keywords)}') # Provide specific recommendations if top_company['total_score'] >= 4: print('‚úÖ HIGH CONFIDENCE - This is very likely the target theater company') print('üîç RECOMMENDED: Search this company\'s website for recent 15th-century productions') elif top_company['total_score'] >= 3: print('‚≠ê GOOD CANDIDATE - Strong match but may need verification') print('üîç RECOMMENDED: Investigate this company\'s programs and recent productions') if productions_found: print(f'‚úÖ Found 15th-century production references at {len(productions_found)} organizations') for prod in productions_found: print(f' ‚Ä¢ {prod["organization"]}: {prod["keywords_found"]}') else: print('‚ö†Ô∏è No 15th-century productions found in homepage content') print('üîç RECOMMENDED: Search production/season pages of top candidates') # Specific next steps based on findings if any('asolo' in company['organization'].lower() for company in analysis_results['companies_found']): print('üéØ ASOLO CONNECTION DETECTED - This is very promising for Italian theater criterion') if any('fsu' in str(company['special_indicators']).lower() for company in analysis_results['companies_found']): print('üéØ FSU CONNECTION DETECTED - This suggests conservatory program') else: print('‚ùå No clear theater company matches found') print('üîç RECOMMENDED: Expand search to additional Sarasota theater organizations') print('üîç ALTERNATIVE: Search for specific venue names (e.g., "Historic Asolo Theater")') print('\n=== SARASOTA THEATER ANALYSIS COMPLETE ===')
